# Task: Kubernetes APF QueueSet Deep-Dive

**Repository:** kubernetes/kubernetes (stripped snapshot)
**Output:** Write your document to `/workspace/documentation.md`

## Objective

Produce an algorithmic deep-dive on APF QueueSet behavior, dispatch flow, and fairness tradeoffs.

## Scope

Focus on the APF QueueSet subsystem.
Your document must explain component responsibilities, end-to-end flow, and extension or operational tradeoffs.

## Content Expectations

Address all of the following in your own structure:
- subsystem purpose, boundaries, and upstream/downstream dependencies
- key components and how responsibilities are split
- end-to-end control/request flow with concrete repository evidence
- failure modes, limits, and design tradeoffs
- extension points, customization hooks, and associated risks
- a concise map of the most important files/directories used in your analysis

## Quality Bar

- Cite concrete file paths from the repository.
- Explain behavior and interactions, not just API signatures.
- Include at least one section on operational implications (performance, reliability, or maintainability).
- Do not fabricate classes, functions, or files.

## Anti-Requirements

- Do not output `doc.go`.
- Do not provide shallow bullet dumps without system flow explanation.
- Do not rely on external docs not present in the workspace.

    27→// QueueSetFactory is used to create QueueSet objects.  Creation, like
    28→// config update, is done in two phases: the first phase consumes the
    29→// QueuingConfig and the second consumes the DispatchingConfig.  They
    30→// are separated so that errors from the first phase can be found
    31→// before committing to a concurrency allotment for the second.
    32→type QueueSetFactory interface {
    33→	// BeginConstruction does the first phase of creating a QueueSet.
    34→	// The RatioedGaugePair observes number of requests,
    35→	// execution covering just the regular phase.
    36→	// The denominator for the waiting phase is
    37→	// max(1, QueuingConfig.QueueLengthLimit) X max(1, QueuingConfig.DesiredNumQueues).
    38→	// The RatioedGauge observes number of seats occupied through all phases of execution.
    39→	// Th

   301	// StartRequest begins the process of handling a request.  We take the
   302	// approach of updating the metrics about total requests queued and
   303	// executing at each point where there is a change in that quantity,
   304	// because the metrics --- and only the metrics --- track that
   305	// quantity per FlowSchema.
   306	// The queueSet's promiseFactory is invoked once if the returned Request is non-nil,
   307	// not invoked if the Request is nil.
   308	func (qs *queueSet) StartRequest(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, hashValue uint64, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}, queueNoteFn fq.QueueNoteFn) (fq.Request, bool) {
   309		qs.lockAndSyncTime(ctx)
   310		defer qs.lock.Unlock()
   311		var req *request
   312	
   313		// ========================================================================
   314		// Step 0:
   315		// Apply only concurrency limit, if zero queues desired
   316		if qs.qCfg.DesiredNumQueues < 1 {
   317			if !qs.canAccommodateSeatsLocked(workEstimate.MaxSeats()) {
   318				klog.V(5).Infof("QS(%s): rejecting request %q %#+v %#+v because %d seats are asked for, %d seats are in use (%d are executing) and the limit is %d",
   319					qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, descr1, descr2, workEstimate, qs.totSeatsInUse, qs.totRequestsExecuting, qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)
   320				qs.totRequestsRejected++
   321				metrics.AddReject(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, "concurrency-limit")
   322				return nil, qs.isIdleLocked()
   323			}
   324			req = qs.dispatchSansQueueLocked(ctx, workEstimate, flowDistinguisher, fsName, descr1, descr2)
   325			return req, false
   326		}
   327

   329		// Step 1:
   330		// 1)

   614	// rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked rejects or enqueues the newly arrived
   615	// request, which has been assigned to a queue.  If up against the
   616	// queue length limit and the concurrency limit then returns false.
   617	// Otherwise enqueues and returns true.
   618	func (qs *queueSet) rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked(request *request) bool {
   619		queue := request.queue
   620		curQueueLength := queue.requestsWaiting.Length()
   621		// rejects the newly arrived request if resource criteria not met
   622		if qs.totSeatsInUse >= qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit &&
   623			curQueueLength >= qs.qCfg.QueueLengthLimit {
   624			return false
   625		}
   626	
   627		qs.enqueueToBoundLocked(request)
   628		return true
   629	}

    23→// removeFromFIFOFunc removes a designated element from the list
    24→// if that element is in the list.
    25→// The complexity of the runtime cost is O(1).
    26→// The returned value is the element removed, if indeed one was removed,
    27→// otherwise `nil`.
    28→type removeFromFIFOFunc func() *request
    29→
    30→// walkFunc is called for each request in the list in the
    31→// oldest -> newest order.
    32→// ok: if walkFunc returns false then the iteration stops immediately.
    33→// walkFunc may remove the given request from the fifo,
    34→// but may not mutate the fifo in any othe way.
    35→type walkFunc func(*request) (ok bool)
    36→
    37→// Internal interface to abstract out the implementation details
    38→// of the underlying list used to maintain the requests.
    39→//
    40→// Note that a fifo, including the removeFromFIFOFuncs returned from Enqueue,
    41→// is not safe for concurrent use by multiple goroutines.
    42→type fifo interface {
    43→	// Enqueue enqu

    23→
    24→// promise implements the WriteOnce interface.
    25→type promise struct {
    26→	doneCtx context.Context
    27→	doneVal interface{}
    28→	setCh   chan struct{}
    29→	onceler sync.Once
    30→	value   interface{}
    31→}
    32→
    33→var _ WriteOnce = &promise{}
    34→
    35→// NewWriteOnce makes a new thread-safe WriteOnce.
    36→//
    37→// If `initial` is non-nil then that value is Set at creation time.
    38→//
    39→// If a `Get` is waiting soon after the channel associated with the
    40→// `doneCtx` becomes selectable (which never happens for the nil
    41→// channel) then `Set(doneVal)` effectively happens at that time.
    42→func NewWriteOnce(initial interface{}, doneCtx context.Context, doneVal interface{}) WriteOnce {
    43→	p := &promise{
    44→		doneCtx: doneCtx,
    45→		doneVal: doneVal,
    46→		setCh:   make(chan struct{}),
    47→	}
    48→	if initial != nil {
    49→		p.Set(initial)
    50→	}
    51→	return p
    52→}
    53→

   399→func (cfgCtlr *configController) updateBorrowingLocked(setCompleters bool, plStates map[string]*priorityLevelState) {
   400→	items := make([]allocProblemItem, 0, len(plStates))
   401→	nonExemptPLNames := make([]string, 0, len(plStates))
   402→	idxOfNonExempt := map[string]int{} // items index of non-exempt classes
   403→	cclOfExempt := map[string]int{}    // minCurrentCL of exempt classes
   404→	var minCLSum, minCurrentCLSum int  // sums over non-exempt classes
   405→	remainingServerCL := cfgCtlr.nominalCLSum
   406→	for plName, plState := range plStates {
   407→		obs := plState.seatDemandIntegrator.Reset()
   408→		plState.seatDemandStats.update(obs)
   409→		var minCurrentCL int
   410→		if plState.pl.Spec.Type == flowcontrol.PriorityLevelEnablementExempt {
   411→			minCurrentCL = max(plState.minCL, plState.seatDemandStats.highWatermark)
   412→			cclOfExempt[plName] = minCurrentCL
   413→			remainingServerCL -= minCurrentCL
   414→		} else {
   415→			// Lower bound on this priority level's adjusted concurreny limit is the lesser of:
   416→			// - its seat demamd high watermark over the last adjustment period, and
   417→			// - its configured concurrency limit.
   418→			// BUT: we do not want this to be lower than the lower bound from configuration.
   419→			// See KEP-1040 for a more detailed explanation.
   420→			minCurrentCL = max(plState.minCL, min(plState.nominalCL, plState.seatDemandStats.highWatermark))
   421→			idxOfNonExempt[plName] = len(items)
   422→			nonExemptPLNames = append(nonExemptPLNames, plName)
   423→			items = append(items, allocProblemItem{
   424→				lowerBound: float64(minCurrentCL),
   425→				upperBound: float64(plState.maxCL),
   426→				target:     math.Max(float64(minCurrentCL), plState.seatDemandStats.smoothed),

    17→package shufflesharding
    18→
    19→import (
    20→	"fmt"
    21→	"math"
    22→)
    23→
    24→// MaxHashBits is the max bit length which can be used from hash value.
    25→// If we use all bits of hash value, the critical(last) card shuffled by
    26→// Dealer will be uneven to 2:3 (first half:second half) at most,
    27→// in order to reduce this unevenness to 32:33, we set MaxHashBits to 60 here.
    28→const MaxHashBits = 60
    29→
    30→// RequiredEntropyBits makes a quick and slightly conservative estimate of the number
    31→// of bits of hash value that are consumed in shuffle sharding a deck of the given size
    32→// to a hand of the given size.  The result is meaningful only if
    33→// 1 <= handSize <= deckSize <= 1<<26.
    34→func RequiredEntropyBits(deckSize, handSize int) int {
    35→	return int(math.Ceil(math.Log2(float64(deckSize)) * float64(handSize)))
    36→}
    37→
    38→// Dealer contains some necessary parameters and provides some methods for shuffle sharding.
    39→// Dealer is thread-safe.
    40→type Dealer struct {
    41→	deckSize int
    42→	hand
... (truncated)

    25→// SeatSeconds is a measure of work, in units of seat-seconds, using a fixed-point representation.
    26→// `SeatSeconds(n)` represents `n/ssScale` seat-seconds.
    27→// The `ssScale` constant is private to the implementation here,
    28→// no other code should use it.
    29→type SeatSeconds uint64
    30→
    31→// MaxSeatsSeconds is the maximum representable value of SeatSeconds
    32→const MaxSeatSeconds = SeatSeconds(math.MaxUint64)
    33→
    34→// MinSeatSeconds is the lowest representable value of SeatSeconds
    35→const MinSeatSeconds = SeatSeconds(0)
    36→
    37→// SeatsTimeDuration produces the SeatSeconds value for the given factors.
    38→// This is intended only to produce small values, increments in work
    39→// rather than amount of work done since process start.
    40→func SeatsTimesDuration(seats float64, duration time.Duration) SeatSeconds {
    41→	return SeatSeconds(int64(math.Round(seats * float64(duration/time.Nanosecond) / (1e9 / ssScale))))
    42→}

    19→// WriteOnce represents a variable that is initially not set and can
    20→// be set once and is readable.  This is the common meaning for
    21→// "promise".
    22→type WriteOnce interface {
    23→	// Get reads the current value of this variable.  If this
    24→	// variable is not set yet then this call blocks until this
    25→	// variable gets a value.
    26→	Get() interface{}
    27→
    28→	// Set normally writes a value into this variable, unblocks every
    29→	// goroutine waiting for this variable to have a value, and
    30→	// returns true.  In the unhappy case that this variable is
    31→	// already set, this method returns false without modifying the
    32→	// variable's value.
    33→	Set(interface{}) bool
    34→}

102-assistanttext-
The document has been written to `/workspace/documentation.md`. Here is a summary of what it covers:

---

**Document structure:**

1. **Subsystem Purpose and Boundaries** — Establishes that each non-exempt priority level owns exactly one QueueSet; defines what is and is not the QueueSet's job; maps upstream dependencies (configController, WorkEstimator, shufflesharding, eventclock) and downstream consumers (Handle, Prometheus, debug endpoint).

2. **Component Responsibilities** — Details each structural piece:
   - `queueSetFactory` / two-phase construction pattern
   - `queueSet` central state machine and its lock-protected fields
   - `queue` per-flow FIFO with aggregated `queueSum`
   - `request` per-request envelope and the `decision` promise
   - `promise.WriteOnce` and its locking contract (Set under lock, Get without lock)
   - `requestFIFO` O(1) closure-based removal
   - `shufflesharding.Dealer` and entropy requirements
   - `configController` and the 10-second borrowing loop
   - `Integrator` for time-weighted seat-demand statistics

3. **End-to-End Request Flow** — Five concrete stages with file+line citations: classification and hash computation, queue assignment via shuffle-sharding, virtual-finish-time dispatch selection, the promise-based goroutine blocking pattern, and two-phase seat release with `AdditionalLatency`.

4. **Fair Queuing Algorithm** — Explains `currentR` / virtual time rate, why `min(seatsRequested, ConcurrencyLimit) / activeQueues` achieves fairness, how `totalWork = InitialSeats×3ms + FinalSeats×AdditionalLatency` weights heavy requests, and the epoch-advancement overflow mechanism.

5. **Failure Modes and Tradeoffs** — Queue-full rejection semantics, oversized-request stall, anti-windup limitations, the hardcoded 3ms estimate problem, 
... (truncated)

The fields listed before the lock\n// should not be changed; the fields listed after the\n// lock must be accessed only while holding the lock.\n//\n// The methods of this type follow the naming convention that the\n// suffix \"Locked\" means the caller must hold the lock; for a method\n// whose name does not end in \"Locked\" either acquires the lock or\n// does not care about locking.\n//\n// The methods of this type also follow the convention that the suffix\n// \"ToBoundLocked\" means that the caller may have to follow up with a\n// call to `boundNextDispatchLocked`.  This is so for a method that\n// changes what request is oldest in a queue, because that change means\n// that the anti-windup hack in boundNextDispatchLocked needs to be\n// applied wrt the revised oldest request in the queue.\ntype queueSet struct {\n\tclock                    eventclock.Interface\n\testimatedServiceDuration time.Duration\n\n\treqsGaugePair metrics.RatioedGaugePair // .RequestsExecuting covers regular phase only\n\n\texecSeatsGauge metrics.RatioedGauge // for all phases of execution\n\n\tseatDemandIntegrator metrics.Gauge\n\n\tpromiseFactory promiseFactory\n\n\tlock sync.Mutex\n\n\t// qCfg holds the current queuing configuration.  Its\n\t// DesiredNumQueues may be less than the current number of queues.\n\t// If its DesiredNumQueues is zero then its other queuing\n\t// parameters retain the settings they had when DesiredNumQueues\n\t// was last non-zero (if ever).\n\tqCfg fq.QueuingConfig\n\n\t// the current dispatching configuration.\n\tdCfg fq.DispatchingConfig\n\n\t// If `qCfg.DesiredNumQueues` is non-zero then dealer is not nil\n\t// and is good for `qCfg`.\n\tdealer *shufflesharding.Dealer\n\n\t// queues may be longer than the desired number, while the excess\n\t// queues are still draining.\n\tqueues []*queue\n\n\t// currentR is the amount of seat-seconds allocated per queue since process startup.\n\t// This is our generalization of the progress meter named R in the original fair queuing work.\n\tcurrentR fqrequest.SeatSeconds\n\n\t// lastRealTime is what `clock.Now()` yielded when `virtualTime` was last updated\n\tlastRealTime time.Time\n\n\t// robinIndex is the index of the last queue dispatched\n\trobinIndex int\n\n\t// totRequestsWaiting is the sum, over all the queues, of the\n\t// number of requests waiting in that queue\n\ttotRequestsWaiting int\n\n\t// totRequestsExecuting is the total number of requests of this\n\t// queueSet that are currently executing.                qsc.factory.clock,\n\t\t\testimatedServiceDuration: 3 * time.Millisecond,\n\t\t\treqsGaugePair:            qsc.reqsGaugePair,\n\t\t\texecSeatsGauge: qCfg.DesiredNumQueues > 0 {\n\t\tqll *= A decision about a request\ntype requestDecision int\n\n// Values passed through a request's decision\nconst (\n\t// Serve this one\n\tdecisionExecute requestDecision = iota\n\n\t// This one's context timed out / was canceled\n\tdecisionCancel\n)\n\n// StartRequest begins the process of handling a request.  We take the\n// approach of updating the metrics about total requests queued and\n// executing at each point where there is a change in that quantity,\n// because the metrics --- and only the metrics --- track that\n// quantity per FlowSchema.\n// The queueSet's promiseFactory is invoked once if the returned Request is non-nil,\n// not invoked if the Request is nil.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) StartRequest(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, hashValue uint64, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}, queueNoteFn fq.QueueNoteFn) (fq.Request, bool) {\n\tqs.lockAndSyncTime(ctx)\n\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n\tvar req *request\n\n\t// ========================================================================\n\t// Step 0:\n\t// Apply only concurrency limit, if zero queues desired\n\tif qs.qCfg.DesiredNumQueues < 1 {\n\t\tif !qs.canAccommodateSeatsLocked(workEstimate.MaxSeats()) {\n\t\t\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): rejecting request %q %#+v %#+v because %d seats are asked for, %d seats are in use (%d are executing) and the limit is %d\",\n\t\t\t\tqs.qCfg.Name, fsName, descr1, descr2, workEstimate, qs.totSeatsInUse, qs.totRequestsExecuting, qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)\n\t\t\tqs.totRequestsRejected++\n\t\t\tmetrics.AddReject(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, \"concurrency-limit\")\n\t\t\treturn nil, qs.isIdleLocked()\n\t\t}\n\t\treq = qs.dispatchSansQueueLocked(ctx, workEstimate, flowDistinguisher, fsName, descr1, descr2)\n\t\treturn req, false\n\t}\n\n\t// ========================================================================\n\t// Step 1:\n\t// 1) Start with shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n\t// 2) Reject current request if there is not enough concurrency shares and\n\t// we are at max queue length\n\t// 3) If not rejected, create a request and enqueue\n\treq = qs.shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked(ctx, workEstimate, hashValue, flowDistinguisher, fsName, descr1, descr2, queueNoteFn)\n\t// req == nil means that the request was rejected - no remaining\n\t// concurrency shares and at max queue length already\n\tif req == nil {\n\t\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): rejecting request %q %#+v %#+v due to queue full\", qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, descr1, descr2)\n\t\tqs.totRequestsRejected++\n\t\tmetrics.AddReject(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, \"queue-full\")\n\t\treturn nil, qs.isIdleLocked()\n\t}\n\n\t// ========================================================================\n\t// Step 2:\n\t// The next step is to invoke the method that dequeues as much\n\t// as possible.\n\t// This method runs a loop, as long as there are non-empty\n\t// queues and the number currently executing is less than the\n\t// assured concurrency value.  The body of the loop uses the\n\t// fair queuing technique to pick a queue and dispatch a\n\t// request from that queue.\n\tqs.dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked()\n\n\treturn req, false\n}\n\n// ordinaryPromiseFactoryFactory is the promiseFactoryFactory that\n// a queueSetFactory would ordinarily use.\n// Test code might use something different.\nfunc ordinaryPromiseFactoryFactory(qs *queueSet) promiseFactory {\n\treturn promise.NewWriteOnce\n}\n\n// MaxSeats returns the maximum number of seats this request requires, it is\n// the maxumum of the two - WorkEstimate.InitialSeats, WorkEstimate.FinalSeats.\nfunc (req *request) MaxSeats() int {\n\treturn req.workEstimate.MaxSeats()\n}\n\nfunc (req *request) InitialSeats() int {\n\treturn int(req.workEstimate.InitialSeats)\n}\n\nfunc (req *request) NoteQueued(inQueue bool) {\n\tif req.queueNoteFn != nil {\n\t\treq.queueNoteFn(inQueue)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (req *request) Finish(execFn func()) bool {\n\texec, idle := req.wait()\n\tif !exec {\n\t\treturn idle\n\t}\n\tfunc() {\n\t\tdefer func() {\n\t\t\tidle = req.qs.finishRequestAndDispatchAsMuchAsPossible(req)\n\t\t}()\n\n\t\texecFn()\n\t}()\n\n\treturn idle\n}\n\nfunc (req *request) wait() (bool, bool) {\n\tqs := req.qs\n\n\t// ========================================================================\n\t// Step 3:\n\t// The final step is to wait on a decision from\n\t// somewhere and then act on it.\n\tdecisionAny := req.decision.Get()\n\tqs.lockAndSyncTime(req.ctx)\n\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n\tif req.waitStarted {\n\t\t// This can not happen, because the client is forbidden to\n\t\t// call Wait twice on the same request\n\t\tklog.Errorf(\"Duplicate call to the Wait method!  Immediately returning execute=false.  QueueSet=%s, startTime=%s, descr1=%#+v, descr2=%#+v\", req.qs.qCfg.Name, req.startTime, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n\t\treturn false, qs.isIdleLocked()\n\t}\n\treq.waitStarted = true\n\tswitch decisionAny {\n\tcase decisionCancel: // handle in code following this switch\n\tcase decisionExecute:\n\t\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): Dispatching request %#+v %#+v from its queue\", qs.qCfg.Name, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n\t\treturn true, false\n\tdefault:\n\t\t// This can not happen, all possible values are handled above\n\t\tklog.Errorf(\"QS(%s): Impossible decision (type %T, value %#+v) for request %#+v %#+v!  Treating as cancel\", qs.qCfg.Name, decisionAny, decisionAny, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n\t}\n\t// TODO(aaron-prindle) add metrics for this case\n\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): Ejecting request %#+v %#+v from its queue\", qs.qCfg.Name, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n\t// remove the request from the queue as its queue wait time has exceeded\n\tqueue := req.queue\n\tif req.removeFromQueueLocked() != nil {\n\t\tdefer qs.boundNextDispatchLocked(queue)\n\t\tqs.totRequestsWaiting--\n\t\tqs.totSeatsWaiting -= req.MaxSeats()\n\t\tqs.totRequestsRejected++\n\t\tqs.totRequestsCancelled++\n\t\tmetrics.AddReject(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, \"time-out\")\n\t\tmetrics.AddRequestsInQueues(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, -1)\n\t\tmetrics.AddSeatsInQueues(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, -req.MaxSeats())\n\t\treq.NoteQueued(false)\n\t\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsWaiting.Add(-1)\n\t\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n\t}\n\treturn false, qs.isIdleLocked()\n}\n\nfunc (qs *queueSet) IsIdle() bool {\n\tqs.lock.Lock()\n\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n\treturn qs.isIdleLocked()\n}\n\nfunc (qs *queueSet) isIdleLocked() bool {\n\treturn qs.totRequestsWaiting == 0 && qs.totRequestsExecuting == 0\n}\n\n// lockAndSyncTime acquires the lock and updates the virtual time.\n// Doing them together avoids the mistake of modifying some queue state\n// before calling syncTimeLocked.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) lockAndSyncTime(ctx context.Context) {\n\tqs.lock.Lock()\n\tqs.syncTimeLocked(ctx)\n}\n\n// syncTimeLocked updates the virtual time based on the assumption\n// that the current state of the queues has been in effect since\n// `qs.lastRealTime`.  Thus, it should be invoked after acquiring the\n// lock and before modifying the state of any queue.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) syncTimeLocked(ctx context.Context) {\n\trealNow := qs.clock.Now()\n\ttimeSinceLast := realNow.Sub(qs.lastRealTime)\n\tqs.lastRealTime = realNow\n\tprevR := qs.currentR\n\tincrR := fqrequest.SeatsTimesDuration(qs.getVirtualTimeRatioLocked(), timeSinceLast)\n\tqs.currentR = prevR + incrR\n\tswitch {\n\tcase prevR > qs.currentR:\n\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"queueset::currentR overflow\"), \"Overflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"when\", realNow.Format(nsTimeFmt), \"prevR\", prevR, \"incrR\", incrR, \"currentR\", qs.currentR)\n\tcase qs.currentR >= highR:\n\t\tqs.advanceEpoch(ctx, realNow, incrR)\n\t}\n\tmetrics.SetCurrentR(qs.qCfg.Name, qs.currentR.ToFloat())\n}\n\n// rDecrement is the amount by which the progress meter R is wound backwards\n// when needed to avoid overflow.\nconst rDecrement = fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds / 2\n\n// highR is the threshold that triggers advance of the epoch.\n// That is, decrementing the global progress meter R by rDecrement.\nconst highR = rDecrement + rDecrement/2\n\n// advanceEpoch subtracts rDecrement from the global progress meter R\n// and all the readings that have been taked from that meter.\n// The now and incrR parameters are only used to add info to the log messages.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) advanceEpoch(ctx context.Context, now time.Time, incrR fqrequest.SeatSeconds) {\n\toldR := qs.currentR\n\tqs.currentR -= rDecrement\n\tklog.InfoS(\"Advancing epoch\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"when\", now.Format(nsTimeFmt), \"oldR\", oldR, \"newR\", qs.currentR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n\tsuccess := true\n\tfor qIdx, queue := range qs.queues {\n\t\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() == 0 && queue.requestsExecuting.Len() == 0 {\n\t\t\t// Do not just decrement, the value could be quite outdated.\n\t\t\t// It is safe to reset to zero in this case, because the next request\n\t\t\t// will overwrite the zero with `qs.currentR`.\n\t\t\tqueue.nextDispatchR = 0\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\toldNextDispatchR := queue.nextDispatchR\n\t\tqueue.nextDispatchR -= rDecrement\n\t\tif queue.nextDispatchR > oldNextDispatchR {\n\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"queue::nextDispatchR underflow\"), \"Underflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"queue\", qIdx, \"oldNextDispatchR\", oldNextDispatchR, \"newNextDispatchR\", queue.nextDispatchR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n\t\t\tsuccess = false\n\t\t}\n\t\tqueue.requestsWaiting.Walk(func(req *request) bool {\n\t\t\toldArrivalR := req.arrivalR\n\t\t\treq.arrivalR -= rDecrement\n\t\t\tif req.arrivalR > oldArrivalR {\n\t\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"request::arrivalR underflow\"), \"Underflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"queue\", qIdx, \"request\", *req, \"oldArrivalR\", oldArrivalR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n\t\t\t\tsuccess = false\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\tmetrics.AddEpochAdvance(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, success)\n}\n\n// getVirtualTimeRatio calculates the rate at which virtual time has\n// been advancing, according to the logic in `doc.go`.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) getVirtualTimeRatioLocked() float64 {\n\tactiveQueues := 0\n\tseatsRequested := 0\n\tfor _, queue := range qs.queues {\n\t\t// here we want the sum of the maximum width of the requests in this queue since our\n\t\t// goal is to find the maximum rate at which the queue could work.\n\t\tseatsRequested += (queue.seatsInUse + queue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum().MaxSeatsSum)\n\t\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() > 0 || queue.requestsExecuting.Len() > 0 {\n\t\t\tactiveQueues++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif activeQueues == 0 {\n\t\treturn 0\n\t}\n\treturn math.Min(float64(seatsRequested), float64(qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)) / float64(activeQueues)\n}\n\n// shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked encapsulates the logic required\n// to validate and enqueue a request for the queueSet/QueueSet:\n// 1) Start with shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n// 2) Reject current request if there is not enough concurrency shares and\n// we are at max queue length\n// 3) If not rejected, create a request and enqueue\n// returns the enqueud request on a successful enqueue\n// returns nil in the case that there is no available concurrency or\n// the queuelengthlimit has been reached\nfunc (qs *queueSet) shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, hashValue uint64, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}, queueNoteFn fq.QueueNoteFn) *request {\n\t// Start with the shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n\tqueueIdx := qs.shuffleShardLocked(hashValue, descr1, descr2)\n\tqueue := qs.queues[queueIdx]\n\n\tdefer qs.boundNextDispatchLocked(queue)\n\n\t// Create a request and enqueue\n\treq := &request{\n\t\tqs:                qs,\n\t\tfsName:            fsName,\n\t\tflowDistinguisher: flowDistinguisher,\n\t\tctx:               ctx,\n\t\tdecision:          qs.promiseFactory(nil, ctx, decisionCancel),\n\t\tarrivalTime:       qs.clock.Now(),\n\t\tarrivalR:          qs.currentR,\n\t\tqueue:             queue,\n\t\tdescr1:            descr1,\n\t\tdescr2:            descr2,\n\t\tqueueNoteFn:       queueNoteFn,\n\t\tworkEstimate:      qs.completeWorkEstimate(workEstimate),\n\t}\n\tif ok := qs.rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked(req); !ok {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tmetrics.ObserveQueueLength(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, queue.requestsWaiting.Length())\n\treturn req\n}\n\n// shuffleShardLocked uses shuffle sharding to select a queue index\n// using the given hashValue and the shuffle sharding parameters of the queueSet.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) shuffleShardLocked(hashValue uint64, descr1, descr2 interface{}) int {\n\tvar backHand [8]int\n\t// Deal into a data structure, so that the order of visit below is not necessarily the order of the deal.\n\t// This removes bias in the case of flows with overlapping hands.\n\thand := qs.dealer.DealIntoHand(hashValue, backHand[:])\n\thandSize := len(hand)\n\toffset := qs.enqueues % handSize\n\tqs.enqueues++\n\tbestQueueIdx := -1\n\tminQueueSeatSeconds := fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds\n\tfor i := 0; i < handSize; i++ {\n\t\tqueueIdx := hand[(offset+i)%handSize]\n\t\tqueue := qs.queues[queueIdx]\n\t\tqueueSum := queue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum()\n\n\t\t// this is the total amount of work in seat-seconds for requests\n\t\t// waiting in this queue, we will select the queue with the minimum.\n\t\tthisQueueSeatSeconds := queueSum.TotalWorkSum\n\t\tklog.V(7).Infof(\"QS(%s): For request %#+v %#+v considering queue %d with sum: %#v and %d seats in use, nextDispatchR=%v\", qs.qCfg.Name, descr1, descr2, queueIdx, queueSum, queue.seatsInUse, queue.nextDispatchR)\n\t\tif thisQueueSeatSeconds < minQueueSeatSeconds {\n\t\t\tminQueueSeatSeconds = thisQueueSeatSeconds\n\t\t\tbestQueueIdx = queueIdx\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif klogV := klog.V(6); klogV.Enabled() {\n\t\tchosenQueue := qs.queues[bestQueueIdx]\n\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: For request %#+v %#+v chose queue %d, with sum: %#v & %d seats in use & nextDispatchR=%v\", qs.qCfg.Name, qs.clock.Now().Format(nsTimeFmt), qs.currentR, descr1, descr2, bestQueueIdx, chosenQueue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum(), chosenQueue.seatsInUse, chosenQueue.nextDispatchR)\n\t}\n\treturn bestQueueIdx\n}\n\n// rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked rejects or enqueues the newly arrived\n// request, which has been assigned to a queue.  If up against the\n// queue length limit and the concurrency limit then returns false.\n// Otherwise enqueues and returns true.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked(request *request) bool {\n\tqueue := request.queue\n\tcurQueueLength := queue.requestsWaiting.Length()\n\t// rejects the newly arrived request if resource criteria not met\n\tif qs.totSeatsInUse >= qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit &&\n\t\tcurQueueLength >= qs.qCfg.QueueLengthLimit {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tqs.enqueueToBoundLocked(request)\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// enqueues a request into its queue.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) enqueueToBoundLocked(request *request) {\n\tqueue := request.queue\n\tnow := qs.clock.Now()\n\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() == 0 && queue.requestsExecuting.Len() == 0 {\n\t\t// the queue\u2019s start R is set to the virtual time.\n\t\tqueue.nextDispatchR = qs.currentR\n\t\tklogV := klog.V(6)\n\t\tif klogV.Enabled() {\n\t\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: initialized queue %d start R due to request %#+v %#+v\", qs.qCfg.Name, now.Format(nsTimeFmt), queue.nextDispatchR, queue.index, request.descr1, request.descr2)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\trequest.removeFromQueueLocked = queue.requestsWaiting.Enqueue(request)\n\tqs.totRequestsWaiting++\n\tqs.totSeatsWaiting += request.MaxSeats()\n\tmetrics.AddRequestsInQueues(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, 1)\n\tmetrics.AddSeatsInQueues(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, request.MaxSeats())\n\trequest.NoteQueued(true)\n\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsWaiting.Add(1)\n\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n}\n\n// dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked does as many dispatches as possible now.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked() {\n\tfor qs.totRequestsWaiting != 0 && qs.totSeatsInUse < qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit && qs.dispatchLocked() {\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (qs *queueSet) dispatchSansQueueLocked(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}) *request {\n\t// does not call metrics.SetDispatchMetrics because there is no queuing and thus no interesting virtual world\n\tnow := qs.clock.Now()\n\treq := &request{\n\t\tqs:                qs,\n\t\tfsName:            fsName,\n\t\tflowDistinguisher: flowDistinguisher,\n\t\tctx:               ctx,\n\t\tstartTime:         now,\n\t\tdecision:          qs.promiseFactory(decisionExecute, ctx, decisionCancel),\n\t\tarrivalTime:       now,\n\t\tarrivalR:          qs.currentR,\n\t\tdescr1:            descr1,\n\t\tdescr2:            descr2,\n\t\tworkEstimate:      qs.completeWorkEstimate(workEstimate),\n\t}\n\tqs.totRequestsExecuting++\n\tqs.totSeatsInUse += req.MaxSeats()\n\tqs.requestsExecutingSet = qs.requestsExecutingSet.Insert(req)\n\tmetrics.AddRequestsExecuting(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, 1)\n\tmetrics.AddSeatConcurrencyInUse(qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, req.MaxSeats())\n\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsExecuting.Add(1)\n\tqs.execSeatsGauge.Add(float64(req.MaxSeats()))\n\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n\tklogV := klog.V(5)\n\tif klogV.Enabled() {\n\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: immediate dispatch of request %q %#+v %#+v, qs will have %d executing\", qs.qCfg.Name, now.Format(nsTimeFmt), qs.currentR, fsName, descr1, descr2, qs.totRequestsExecuting)\n\t}\n\treturn req\n}\n\n// dispatchLocked uses the Fair Queuing for Server Requests method to\n// select a queue and dispatch the oldest request in that queue.  The\n// return value indicates whether a request was dequeued; this will\n// be false when either all queues are empty or the request at the head\n// of the next queue cannot be dispatched.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) dispatchLocked() bool {\n\tqueue, request := qs.findDispatchQueueToBoundLocked()\n\tif queue == nil {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\tif request == nil { // This should never happen.  But if it does...\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\tqs.totRequestsWaiting--\n\tqs.totSeatsWaiting -= request.MaxSeats()\n\tmetrics.AddRequestsInQueues(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, -1)\n\tmetrics.AddSeatsInQueues(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, -request.MaxSeats())\n\trequest.NoteQueued(false)\n\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsWaiting.Add(-1)\n\tdefer qs.boundNextDispatchLocked(queue)\n\tif !request.decision.Set(decisionExecute) {\n\t\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\trequest.startTime = qs.clock.Now()\n\t// At this moment the request leaves its queue and starts\n\t// executing.  We do not recognize any interim state between\n\t// \"queued\" and \"executing\".  While that means \"executing\"\n\t// includes a little overhead from this package, this is not a\n\t// problem because other overhead is also included.\n\tqs.totRequestsExecuting++\n\tqs.totSeatsInUse += request.MaxSeats()\n\tqueue.requestsExecuting = queue.requestsExecuting.Insert(request)\n\tqueue.seatsInUse += request.MaxSeats()\n\tmetrics.AddRequestsExecuting(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, 1)\n\tmetrics.AddSeatConcurrencyInUse(qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, request.MaxSeats())\n\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsExecuting.Add(1)\n\tqs.execSeatsGauge.Add(float64(request.MaxSeats()))\n\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n\tklogV := klog.V(6)\n\tif klogV.Enabled() {\n\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: dispatching request %#+v %#+v work %v from queue %d with start R %v, queue will have %d waiting & %d requests occupying %d seats, set will have %d seats occupied\",\n\t\t\tqs.qCfg.Name, request.startTime.Format(nsTimeFmt), qs.currentR, request.descr1, request.descr2,\n\t\t\trequest.workEstimate, queue.index, queue.nextDispatchR, queue.requestsWaiting.Length(), queue.requestsExecuting.Len(), queue.seatsInUse, qs.totSeatsInUse)\n\t}\n\t// When a request is dequeued for service -> qs.virtualStart += G * width\n\tif request.totalWork() > rDecrement/100 { // A single increment should never be so big\n\t\tklog.Errorf(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: dispatching request %#+v %#+v with implausibly high work %v from queue %d with start R %v\",\n\t\t\tqs.qCfg.Name, request.startTime.Format(nsTimeFmt), qs.currentR, request.descr1, request.descr2,\n\t\t\trequest.workEstimate, queue.index, queue.nextDispatchR)\n\t}\n\tqueue.nextDispatchR += request.totalWork()\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// canAccommodateSeatsLocked returns true if this queueSet has enough\n// seats available to accommodate a request with the given number of seats,\n// otherwise it returns false.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) canAccommodateSeatsLocked(seats int) bool {\n\tswitch {\n\tcase qs.qCfg.DesiredNumQueues < 0:\n\t\t// This is code for exemption from limitation\n\t\treturn true\n\tcase seats > qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit:\n\t\t// we have picked the queue with the minimum virtual finish time, but\n\t\t// the number of seats this request asks for exceeds the concurrency limit.\n\t\t// TODO: this is a quick fix for now, once we have borrowing in place we will not need it\n\t\tif qs.totRequestsExecuting == 0 {\n\t\t\t// TODO: apply additional lateny associated with this request, as described in the KEP\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t\t// wait for all \"currently\" executing requests in this queueSet\n\t\t// to finish before we can execute this request.\n\t\treturn false\n\tcase qs.totSeatsInUse+seats > qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit:\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// findDispatchQueueToBoundLocked examines the queues in round robin order and\n// returns the first one of those for which the virtual finish time of\n// the oldest waiting request is minimal, and also returns that request.\n// Returns nils if the head of the selected queue can not be dispatched now,\n// in which case the caller does not need to follow up with`qs.boundNextDispatchLocked`.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) findDispatchQueueToBoundLocked() (*queue, *request) {\n\tminVirtualFinish := fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds\n\tsMin := fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds\n\tdsMin := fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds\n\tsMax := fqrequest.MinSeatSeconds\n\tdsMax := fqrequest.MinSeatSeconds\n\tvar minQueue *queue\n\tvar minIndex int\n\tnq := len(qs.queues)\n\tfor range qs.queues {\n\t\tqs.robinIndex = (qs.robinIndex + 1) % nq\n\t\tqueue := qs.queues[qs.robinIndex]\n\t\toldestWaiting, _ := queue.requestsWaiting.Peek()\n\t\tif oldestWaiting != nil {\n\t\t\tsMin = min(sMin, queue.nextDispatchR)\n\t\t\tsMax = max(sMax, queue.nextDispatchR)\n\t\t\testimatedWorkInProgress := fqrequest.SeatsTimesDuration(float64(queue.seatsInUse), qs.estimatedServiceDuration)\n\t\t\tdsMin = min(dsMin, queue.nextDispatchR-estimatedWorkInProgress)\n\t\t\tdsMax = max(dsMax, queue.nextDispatchR-estimatedWorkInProgress)\n\t\t\tcurrentVirtualFinish := queue.nextDispatchR + oldestWaiting.totalWork()\n\t\t\tklog.V(11).InfoS(\"Considering queue to dispatch\", \"queueSet\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"queue\", qs.robinIndex, \"finishR\", currentVirtualFinish)\n\t\t\tif currentVirtualFinish < minVirtualFinish {\n\t\t\t\tminVirtualFinish = currentVirtualFinish\n\t\t\t\tminQueue = queue\n\t\t\t\tminIndex = qs.robinIndex\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\toldestReqFromMinQueue, _ := minQueue.requestsWaiting.Peek()\n\tif oldestReqFromMinQueue == nil {\n\t\t// This cannot happen\n\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"selected queue is empty\"), \"Impossible\", \"queueSet\", qs.qCfg.Name)\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\tif !qs.canAccommodateSeatsLocked(oldestReqFromMinQueue.MaxSeats()) {\n\t\t// since we have not picked the queue with the minimum virtual finish\n\t\t// time, we are not going to advance the round robin index here.\n\t\tklogV := klog.V(4)\n\t\tif klogV.Enabled() {\n\t\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s): request %v %v seats %d cannot be dispatched from queue %d, waiting for currently executing requests to complete, %d requests are occupying %d seats and the limit is %d\",\n\t\t\t\tqs.qCfg.Name, oldestReqFromMinQueue.descr1, oldestReqFromMinQueue.descr2, oldestReqFromMinQueue.MaxSeats(), minQueue.index, qs.totRequestsExecuting, qs.totSeatsInUse, qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)\n\t\t}\n\t\tmetrics.AddDispatchWithNoAccommodation(qs.qCfg.Name, oldestReqFromMinQueue.fsName)\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\toldestReqFromMinQueue.removeFromQueueLocked()\n\n\t// If the requested final seats exceed capacity of that queue,\n\t// we reduce them to current capacity and adjust additional latency\n\t// to preserve the total amount of work.\n\tif oldestReqFromMinQueue.workEstimate.FinalSeats > uint64(qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit) {\n\t\tfinalSeats := uint64(qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)\n\t\tadditionalLatency := oldestReqFromMinQueue.workEstimate.finalWork.DurationPerSeat(float64(finalSeats))\n\t\toldestReqFromMinQueue.workEstimate.FinalSeats = finalSeats\n\t\toldestReqFromMinQueue.workEstimate.AdditionalLatency = additionalLatency\n\t}\n\n\t// we set the round robin indexing to start at the chose queue\n\t// for the next round. This\n// callback updates important state in the queueSet\nfunc (qs *queueSet) finishRequestLocked(r *request) {\n\tnow := 223\u2192\t\t}\n   224\u2192\t\tqs.promiseFactory = qsc.factory.promiseFactoryFactory(qs)\n   225\u2192\t}\n   226\u2192\tqs.setConfiguration(context.Background(), qsc.qCfg, qsc.dealer, dCfg)\n   227\u2192\treturn qs\n   228\u2192}\n   229\u2192\n   230\u2192// createQueues is a helper method for initializing an array of n queues\n   231\u2192func createQueues(n, baseIndex int) []*queue {\n   232\u2192\tfqqueues := make([]*queue, n)\n   233\u2192\tfor i := 0; i < n; i++ {\n   234\u2192\t\tfqqueues[i] = &queue{index: baseIndex + i, requestsWaiting: newRequestFIFO(), requestsExecuting: sets.New[*request]()}\n   235\u2192\t}\n   236\u2192\treturn fqqueues\n   237\u2192}\n   238\u2192\n   239\u2192func (qs *queueSet) BeginConfigChange(qCfg fq.QueuingConfig) (fq.QueueSetCompleter, error) {\n   240\u2192\tdealer, err := checkConfig(qCfg)\n   241\u2192\tif err != nil {\n   242\u2192\t\treturn nil, err\n   243\u2192\t}\n   244\u2192\treturn &queueSetCompleter{\n   245\u2192\t\ttheSet: qs,\n   246\u2192\t\tqCfg:   qCfg,\n   247\u2192\t\tdealer: dealer}, nil\n   248\u2192}\n   249\u2192\n   250\u2192// setConfiguration is used to set the configuration for a queueSet.\n   251\u2192// Update handling for when fields are updated is handled here as well -\n   252\u2192// eg: if DesiredNum is increased, setConfiguration reconciles by\n   253\u2192// adding more queues.\n   254\u2192func (qs *queueSet) setConfiguration(ctx context.Context, qCfg fq.QueuingConfig, dealer *shufflesharding.Dealer, dCfg fq.DispatchingConfig) {\n   255\u2192\tqs.lockAndSyncTime(ctx)\n   256\u2192\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n   257\u2192\n   258\u2192\tif qCfg.DesiredNumQueues > 0 {\n   259\u2192\t\t// Adding queues is the only thing that requires immediate action\n   260\u2192\t\t// Removing queues is handled by attrition, removing a queue when\n   261\u2192\t\t// it goes empty and there are too many.\n   262\u2192\t\tnumQueues := 271\u2192\n   272\u2192\tqs.qCfg = qCfg\n   273\u2192\tqs.dCfg = dCfg\n   274\u2192\tqs.dealer = dealer\n   275\u2192\tqll := qCfg.QueueLengthLimit\n   276\u2192\tif qll < 1 {\n   277\u2192\t\tqll = 282\u2192\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsWaiting.SetDenominator(float64(qll))\n   283\u2192\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsExecuting.SetDenominator(float64(dCfg.ConcurrencyDenominator))\n   284\u2192\tqs.execSeatsGauge.SetDenominator(float64(dCfg.ConcurrencyDenominator))\n   285\u2192\n   286\u2192\tqs.dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked()\n   287\u2192}\n   288\u2192\n   289\u2192// A decision about a request\n   290\u2192type requestDecision int\n   291\u2192\n   292\u2192// Values passed through a request's decision\n   293\u2192const (\n   294\u2192\t// Serve this one\n   295\u2192\tdecisionExecute requestDecision = iota\n   296\u2192\n   297\u2192\t// This one's context timed out / was canceled\n   298\u2192\tdecisionCancel\n   299\u2192)\n   300\u2192\n   301\u2192// StartRequest begins the process of handling a request.  We take the\n   302\u2192// approach of updating the metrics about total requests queued and\n   303\u2192// executing at each point where there is a change in that quantity,\n   304\u2192// because the metrics --- and only the metrics --- track that\n   305\u2192// quantity per FlowSchema.\n   306\u2192// The queueSet's promiseFactory is invoked once if the returned Request is non-nil,\n   307\u2192// not invoked if the Request is nil.\n   308\u2192func (qs *queueSet) StartRequest(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, hashValue uint64, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}, queueNoteFn fq.QueueNoteFn) (fq.Request, bool) {\n   309\u2192\tqs.lockAndSyncTime(ctx)\n   310\u2192\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n   311\u2192\tvar req *request\n   312\u2192\n   313\u2192\t// ========================================================================\n   314\u2192\t// Step 0:\n   315\u2192\t// Apply only concurrency limit, if zero queues desired\n   316\u2192\tif qs.qCfg.DesiredNumQueues < 1 {\n   317\u2192\t\tif !qs.canAccommodateSeatsLocked(workEstimate.MaxSeats()) {\n   318\u2192\t\t\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): rejecting request %q %#+v %#+v because %d seats are asked for, %d seats are in use (%d are executing) and the limit is %d\",\n   319\u2192\t\t\t\tqs.qCfg.Name, fsName, descr1, descr2, workEstimate, qs.totSeatsInUse, 322\u2192\t\t\treturn nil, qs.isIdleLocked()\n   323\u2192\t\t}\n   324\u2192\t\treq = qs.dispatchSansQueueLocked(ctx, workEstimate, flowDistinguisher, fsName, descr1, descr2)\n   325\u2192\t\treturn req, false\n   326\u2192\t}\n   327\u2192\n   328\u2192\t// ========================================================================\n   329\u2192\t// Step 1:\n   330\u2192\t// 1) Start with shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n   331\u2192\t// 2) Reject current request if there is not enough concurrency shares and\n   332\u2192\t// we are at max queue length\n   333\u2192\t// 3) If not rejected, create a request and enqueue\n   334\u2192\treq = qs.shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked(ctx, workEstimate, hashValue, flowDistinguisher, fsName, descr1, descr2, queueNoteFn)\n   335\u2192\t// req == nil means that the request was rejected - no remaining\n   336\u2192\t// concurrency shares and at max queue length already\n   337\u2192\tif req == nil {\n   338\u2192\t\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): rejecting request %q %#+v %#+v due to queue full\", qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, descr1, descr2)\n   339\u2192\t\tqs.totRequestsRejected++\n   340\u2192\t\tmetrics.AddReject(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, \"queue-full\")\n   341\u2192\t\treturn nil, qs.isIdleLocked()\n   342\u2192\t}\n   343\u2192\n   344\u2192\t// ========================================================================\n   345\u2192\t// Step 2:\n   346\u2192\t// The next step is to invoke the method that dequeues as much\n   347\u2192\t// as possible.\n   348\u2192\t// This method runs a loop, as long as there are non-empty\n   349\u2192\t// queues and the number currently executing is less than the\n   350\u2192\t// assured concurrency value.  The body of the loop uses the\n   351\u2192\t// fair queuing technique to pick a queue and dispatch a\n   352\u2192\t// request from that queue.\n   353\u2192\tqs.dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked()\n   354\u2192\n   355\u2192\treturn req, false\n   356\u2192}\n   357\u2192\n   358\u2192// ordinaryPromiseFactoryFactory is the promiseFactoryFactory that\n   359\u2192// a queueSetFactory would ordinarily use.\n   360\u2192// Test code might use something different.\n   361\u2192func ordinaryPromiseFactoryFactory(qs *queueSet) promiseFactory {\n   362\u2192\treturn promise.NewWriteOnce\n   363\u2192}\n   364\u2192\n   365\u2192// MaxSeats returns the maximum number of seats this request requires, it is\n   366\u2192// the maxumum of the two - Immediately returning execute=false.  QueueSet=%s, startTime=%s, descr1=%#+v, descr2=%#+v\", req.qs.qCfg.Name, req.startTime, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n   411\u2192\t\treturn false, qs.isIdleLocked()\n   412\u2192\t}\n   413\u2192\treq.waitStarted = true\n   414\u2192\tswitch decisionAny {\n   415\u2192\tcase decisionCancel: // handle in code following this switch\n   416\u2192\tcase decisionExecute:\n   417\u2192\t\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): Dispatching request %#+v %#+v from its queue\", qs.qCfg.Name, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n   418\u2192\t\treturn true, false\n   419\u2192\tdefault:\n   420\u2192\t\t// This can not happen, all possible values are handled above\n   421\u2192\t\tklog.Errorf(\"QS(%s): Impossible decision (type %T, value %#+v) for request %#+v %#+v!  Treating as cancel\", qs.qCfg.Name, decisionAny, decisionAny, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n   422\u2192\t}\n   423\u2192\t// TODO(aaron-prindle) add metrics for this case\n   424\u2192\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): Ejecting request %#+v %#+v from its queue\", qs.qCfg.Name, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n   425\u2192\t// remove the request from the queue as its queue wait time has exceeded\n   426\u2192\tqueue := req.queue\n   427\u2192\tif req.removeFromQueueLocked() != nil {\n   428\u2192\t\tdefer qs.boundNextDispatchLocked(queue)\n   429\u2192\t\tqs.totRequestsWaiting--\n   430\u2192\t\tqs.totSeatsWaiting -= req.MaxSeats()\n   431\u2192\t\tqs.totRequestsRejected++\n   432\u2192\t\tqs.totRequestsCancelled++\n   433\u2192\t\tmetrics.AddReject(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, \"time-out\")\n   434\u2192\t\tmetrics.AddRequestsInQueues(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, -1)\n   435\u2192\t\tmetrics.AddSeatsInQueues(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, -req.MaxSeats())\n   436\u2192\t\treq.NoteQueued(false)\n   437\u2192\t\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsWaiting.Add(-1)\n   438\u2192\t\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n   439\u2192\t}\n   440\u2192\treturn false, qs.isIdleLocked()\n   441\u2192}\n   442\u2192\n   443\u2192func (qs *queueSet) IsIdle() bool {\n   444\u2192\tqs.lock.Lock()\n   445\u2192\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n   446\u2192\treturn qs.isIdleLocked()\n   447\u2192}\n   448\u2192\n   449\u2192func (qs *queueSet) isIdleLocked() bool {\n   450\u2192\treturn qs.totRequestsWaiting == 0 && qs.totRequestsExecuting == 0\n   451\u2192}\n   452\u2192\n   453\u2192// lockAndSyncTime acquires the lock and updates the virtual time.\n   454\u2192// Doing them together avoids the mistake of modifying some queue state\n   455\u2192// before calling syncTimeLocked.\n   456\u2192func (qs *queueSet) lockAndSyncTime(ctx context.Context) {\n   457\u2192\tqs.lock.Lock()\n   458\u2192\tqs.syncTimeLocked(ctx)\n   459\u2192}\n   460\u2192\n   461\u2192// syncTimeLocked updates the virtual time based on the assumption\n   462\u2192// that the current state of the queues has been in effect since\n   463\u2192// `qs.lastRealTime`.  Thus, it should be invoked after acquiring the\n   464\u2192// lock and before modifying the state of any queue.\n   465\u2192func (qs *queueSet) syncTimeLocked(ctx context.Context) {\n   466\u2192\trealNow := qs.clock.Now()\n   467\u2192\ttimeSinceLast := realNow.Sub(qs.lastRealTime)\n   468\u2192\tqs.lastRealTime = realNow\n   469\u2192\tprevR := qs.currentR\n   470\u2192\tincrR := fqrequest.SeatsTimesDuration(qs.getVirtualTimeRatioLocked(), timeSinceLast)\n   471\u2192\tqs.currentR = prevR + incrR\n   472\u2192\tswitch {\n   473\u2192\tcase prevR > qs.currentR:\n   474\u2192\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"queueset::currentR overflow\"), \"Overflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"when\", realNow.Format(nsTimeFmt), \"prevR\", prevR, \"incrR\", incrR, \"currentR\", qs.currentR)\n   475\u2192\tcase qs.currentR >= highR:\n   476\u2192\t\tqs.advanceEpoch(ctx, realNow, incrR)\n   477\u2192\t}\n   478\u2192\tmetrics.SetCurrentR(qs.qCfg.Name, qs.currentR.ToFloat())\n   479\u2192}\n   480\u2192\n   481\u2192// rDecrement is the amount by which the progress meter R is wound backwards\n   482\u2192// when needed to avoid overflow.\n   483\u2192const rDecrement = fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds / 2\n   484\u2192\n   485\u2192// highR is the threshold that triggers advance of the epoch.\n   486\u2192// That is, decrementing the global progress meter R by rDecrement.\n   487\u2192const highR = rDecrement + rDecrement/2\n   488\u2192\n   489\u2192// advanceEpoch subtracts rDecrement from the global progress meter R\n   490\u2192// and all the readings that have been taked from that meter.\n   491\u2192// The now and incrR parameters are only used to add info to the log messages.\n   492\u2192func (qs *queueSet) advanceEpoch(ctx context.Context, now time.Time, incrR fqrequest.SeatSeconds) {\n   493\u2192\toldR := qs.currentR\n   494\u2192\tqs.currentR -= rDecrement\n   495\u2192\tklog.InfoS(\"Advancing epoch\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"when\", now.Format(nsTimeFmt), \"oldR\", oldR, \"newR\", qs.currentR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n   496\u2192\tsuccess := true\n   497\u2192\tfor qIdx, queue := range qs.queues {\n   498\u2192\t\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() == 0 && queue.requestsExecuting.Len() == 0 {\n   499\u2192\t\t\t// Do not just decrement, the value could be quite outdated.\n   500\u2192\t\t\t// It is safe to reset to zero in this case, because the next request\n   501\u2192\t\t\t// will overwrite the zero with `qs.currentR`.\n   502\u2192\t\t\tqueue.nextDispatchR = 0\n   503\u2192\t\t\tcontinue\n   504\u2192\t\t}\n   505\u2192\t\toldNextDispatchR := queue.nextDispatchR\n   506\u2192\t\tqueue.nextDispatchR -= rDecrement\n   507\u2192\t\tif queue.nextDispatchR > oldNextDispatchR {\n   508\u2192\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"queue::nextDispatchR underflow\"), \"Underflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"queue\", qIdx, \"oldNextDispatchR\", oldNextDispatchR, \"newNextDispatchR\", queue.nextDispatchR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n   509\u2192\t\t\tsuccess = false\n   510\u2192\t\t}\n   511\u2192\t\tqueue.requestsWaiting.Walk(func(req *request) bool {\n   512\u2192\t\t\toldArrivalR := req.arrivalR\n   513\u2192\t\t\treq.arrivalR -= rDecrement\n   514\u2192\t\t\tif req.arrivalR > oldArrivalR {\n   515\u2192\t\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"request::arrivalR underflow\"), \"Underflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"queue\", qIdx, \"request\", *req, \"oldArrivalR\", oldArrivalR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n   516\u2192\t\t\t\tsuccess = false\n   517\u2192\t\t\t}\n   518\u2192\t\t\treturn true\n   519\u2192\t\t})\n   520\u2192\t}\n   521\u2192\tmetrics.AddEpochAdvance(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, success)\n   522\u2192}\n   523\u2192\n   524\u2192// getVirtualTimeRatio calculates the rate at which virtual time has\n   525\u2192// been advancing, according to the logic in `doc.go`.\n   526\u2192func (qs *queueSet) getVirtualTimeRatioLocked() float64 {\n   527\u2192\tactiveQueues := 0\n   528\u2192\tseatsRequested := 0\n   529\u2192\tfor _, queue := range qs.queues {\n   530\u2192\t\t// here we want the sum of the maximum width of the requests in this queue since our\n   531\u2192\t\t// goal is to find the maximum rate at which the queue could work.\n   532\u2192\t\tseatsRequested += (queue.seatsInUse + queue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum().MaxSeatsSum)\n   533\u2192\t\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() > 0 || queue.requestsExecuting.Len() > 0 {\n   534\u2192\t\t\tactiveQueues++\n   535\u2192\t\t}\n   536\u2192\t}\n   537\u2192\tif activeQueues == 0 {\n   538\u2192\t\treturn 0\n   539\u2192\t}\n   540\u2192\treturn math.Min(float64(seatsRequested), float64(qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)) / float64(activeQueues)\n   541\u2192}\n   542\u2192\n   543\u2192// shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked encapsulates the logic required\n   544\u2192// to validate and enqueue a request for the queueSet/QueueSet:\n   545\u2192// 1) Start with shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n   546\u2192// 2) Reject current request if there is not enough concurrency shares and\n   547\u2192// we are at max queue length\n   548\u2192// 3) If not rejected, create a request and enqueue\n   549\u2192// returns the enqueud request on a successful enqueue\n   550\u2192// returns nil in the case that there is no available concurrency or\n   551\u2192// the queuelengthlimit has been reached\n   552\u2192func (qs *queueSet) shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, hashValue uint64, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}, queueNoteFn fq.QueueNoteFn) *request {\n   553\u2192\t// Start with the shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n   554\u2192\tqueueIdx := qs.shuffleShardLocked(hashValue, descr1, descr2)\n   555\u2192\tqueue := qs.queues[queueIdx]\n   556\u2192\n   557\u2192\tdefer qs.boundNextDispatchLocked(queue)\n   558\u2192\n   559\u2192\t// Create a request and enqueue\n   560\u2192\treq := &request{\n   561\u2192\t\tqs:                qs,\n   562\u2192\t\tfsName:            fsName,\n   563\u2192\t\tflowDistinguisher: flowDistinguisher,\n   564\u2192\t\tctx:               ctx,\n   565\u2192\t\tdecision:          qs.promiseFactory(nil, ctx, decisionCancel),\n   566\u2192\t\tarrivalTime:       qs.clock.Now(),\n   567\u2192\t\tarrivalR:          qs.currentR,\n   568\u2192\t\tqueue:             queue,\n   569\u2192\t\tdescr1:            descr1,\n   570\u2192\t\tdescr2:            descr2,\n   571\u2192\t\tqueueNoteFn:       queueNoteFn,\n   572\u2192\t\tworkEstimate:      qs.completeWorkEstimate(workEstimate),\n   573\u2192\t}\n   574\u2192\tif ok := qs.rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked(req); !ok {\n   575\u2192\t\treturn nil\n   576\u2192\t}\n   577\u2192\tmetrics.ObserveQueueLength(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, queue.requestsWaiting.Length())\n   578\u2192\treturn req\n   579\u2192}\n   580\u2192\n   581\u2192// shuffleShardLocked uses shuffle sharding to select a queue index\n   582\u2192// using the given hashValue and the shuffle sharding parameters of the queueSet.\n   583\u2192func (qs *queueSet) shuffleShardLocked(hashValue uint64, descr1, descr2 interface{}) int {\n   584\u2192\tvar backHand [8]int\n   585\u2192\t// Deal into a data structure, so that the order of visit below is not necessarily the order of the deal.\n   586\u2192\t// This removes bias in the case of flows with overlapping hands.\n   587\u2192\thand := qs.dealer.DealIntoHand(hashValue, backHand[:])\n   588\u2192\thandSize := len(hand)\n   589\u2192\toffset := qs.enqueues % handSize\n   590\u2192\tqs.enqueues++\n   591\u2192\tbestQueueIdx := -1\n   592\u2192\tminQueueSeatSeconds := fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds\n   593\u2192\tfor i := 0; i < handSize; i++ {\n   594\u2192\t\tqueueIdx := hand[(offset+i)%handSize]\n   595\u2192\t\tqueue := qs.queues[queueIdx]\n   596\u2192\t\tqueueSum := queue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum()\n   597\u2192\n   598\u2192\t\t// this is the total amount of work in seat-seconds for requests\n   599\u2192\t\t// waiting in this queue, we will select the queue with the minimum.\n   600\u2192\t\tthisQueueSeatSeconds := queueSum.TotalWorkSum\n   601\u2192\t\tklog.V(7).Infof(\"QS(%s): For request %#+v %#+v thisQueueSeatSeconds < minQueueSeatSeconds {\n   603\u2192\t\t\tminQueueSeatSeconds = thisQueueSeatSeconds\n   604\u2192\t\t\tbestQueueIdx = queueIdx\n   605\u2192\t\t}\n   606\u2192\t}\n newly arrived\n   615\u2192// request, which has been assigned to a queue.  If up against the\n   616\u2192// queue length limit and the concurrency limit then returns false.\n   617\u2192// Otherwise enqueues and returns true.\n   618\u2192func (qs *queueSet) rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked(request *request) bool {\n   619\u2192\tqueue := request.queue\n   620\u2192\tcurQueueLength := queue.requestsWaiting.Length()\n   621\u2192\t// rejects the newly arrived request if resource criteria not met\n   622\u2192\tif qs.totSeatsInUse >= qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit &&\n   623\u2192\t\tcurQueueLength >= qs.qCfg.QueueLengthLimit {\n   624\u2192\t\treturn false\n   625\u2192\t}\n   626\u2192\n   627\u2192\tqs.enqueueToBoundLocked(request)\n   628\u2192\treturn true\n   629\u2192}\n   630\u2192\n   631\u2192// enqueues a request into its queue.\n   632\u2192func (qs *queueSet) enqueueToBoundLocked(request *request) {\n   633\u2192\tqueue := request.queue\n   634\u2192\tnow := qs.clock.Now()\n   635\u2192\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() == 0 && queue.requestsExecuting.Len() == 0 {\n   636\u2192\t\t// the queue\u2019s start R is set to the virtual time.\n   637\u2192\t\tqueue.nextDispatchR = qs.currentR\n   638\u2192\t\tklogV := klog.V(6)\n   639\u2192\t\tif klogV.Enabled() {\n   640\u2192\t\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: initialized queue %d start R due to request %#+v %#+v\", qs.qCfg.Name, now.Format(nsTimeFmt), queue.nextDispatchR, queue.index, request.descr1, request.descr2)\n   641\u2192\t\t}\n   642\u2192\t}\n   643\u2192\trequest.removeFromQueueLocked = queue.requestsWaiting.Enqueue(request)\n 647\u2192\tmetrics.AddSeatsInQueues(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, request.MaxSeats())\n   648\u2192\trequest.NoteQueued(true)\n   649\u2192\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsWaiting.Add(1)\n   650\u2192\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n   651\u2192}\n   652\u2192\n   653\u2192// dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked does as many dispatches as possible now.\n   654\u2192func (qs *queueSet) dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked() {\n   655\u2192\tfor qs.totRequestsWaiting != 0 && qs.totSeatsInUse < qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit && qs.dispatchLocked() {\n   656\u2192\t}\n   657\u2192}\n   658\u2192\n   659\u2192func (qs *queueSet) dispatchSansQueueLocked(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}) *request {\n   660\u2192\t// does not call metrics.SetDispatchMetrics because there is no queuing and thus no interesting virtual world\n   661\u2192\tnow := qs.clock.Now()\n   662\u2192\treq := &request{\n   663\u2192\t\tqs:                qs,\n   664\u2192\t\tfsName:            fsName,\n   665\u2192\t\tflowDistinguisher: flowDistinguisher,\n   666\u2192\t\tctx:               ctx,\n   667\u2192\t\tstartTime:         now,\n   668\u2192\t\tdecision:          qs.promiseFactory(decisionExecute, ctx, decisionCancel),\n   669\u2192\t\tarrivalTime:       now,\n 690\u2192// dispatchLocked uses the Fair Queuing for Server Requests method to\n   691\u2192// select a queue and dispatch the oldest request in that queue.  The\n   692\u2192// return value indicates whether a request was dequeued; this will\n   693\u2192// be false when either all queues are empty or the request at the head\n   694\u2192// of the next queue cannot be dispatched.\n   695\u2192func (qs *queueSet) dispatchLocked() bool {\n   696\u2192\tqueue, request := qs.findDispatchQueueToBoundLocked()\n   697\u2192\tif queue == nil {\n   698\u2192\t\treturn false\n   699\u2192\t}\n   700\u2192\tif request == nil { // This should never happen.  But if it does...\n   701\u2192\t\treturn false\n   702\u2192\t}\n   703\u2192\tqs.totRequestsWaiting--\n   704\u2192\tqs.totSeatsWaiting -= request.MaxSeats()\n   705\u2192\tmetrics.AddRequestsInQueues(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, -1)\n   706\u2192\tmetrics.AddSeatsInQueues(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, -request.MaxSeats())\n   707\u2192\trequest.NoteQueued(false)\n   708\u2192\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsWaiting.Add(-1)\n   709\u2192\tdefer qs.boundNextDispatchLocked(queue)\n   710\u2192\tif !request.decision.Set(decisionExecute) {\n   711\u2192\t\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n   712\u2192\t\treturn true\n   713\u2192\t}\n   714\u2192\trequest.startTime = qs.clock.Now()\n   715\u2192\t// At this moment the request leaves its queue and starts\n   716\u2192\t// executing.  We do not recognize any interim state between\n   717\u2192\t// \"queued\" and \"executing\".  While that means \"executing\"\n   718\u2192\t// includes a little overhead from this package, this is not a\n   719\u2192\t// problem because other overhead is also included.\n   720\u2192\tqs.totRequestsExecuting++\n   721\u2192\tqs.totSeatsInUse += request.MaxSeats()\n   722\u2192\tqueue.requestsExecuting = queue.requestsExecuting.Insert(request)\n   723\u2192\tqueue.seatsInUse += request.MaxSeats()\n   724\u2192\tmetrics.AddRequestsExecuting(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, 1)\n   725\u2192\tmetrics.AddSeatConcurrencyInUse(qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, request.MaxSeats())\n   726\u2192\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsExecuting.Add(1)\n   727\u2192\tqs.execSeatsGauge.Add(float64(request.MaxSeats()))\n   728\u2192\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n   729\u2192\tklogV := klog.V(6)\n   730\u2192\tif klogV.Enabled() {\n   731\u2192\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: dispatching request %#+v %#+v work %v from queue %d with start R %v, queue will have %d waiting & %d requests occupying %d seats, set will have %d seats occupied\",\n   732\u2192\t\t\tqs.qCfg.Name, request.startTime.Format(nsTimeFmt), qs.currentR, request.descr1, request.descr2,\n   733\u2192\t\t\trequest.workEstimate, queue.index, queue.nextDispatchR, width\n   736\u2192\tif request.totalWork() > rDecrement/100 { // A single increment should never be so big\n   737\u2192\t\tklog.Errorf(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: dispatching request %#+v %#+v with 739\u2192\t\t\trequest.workEstimate, queue.index, queue.nextDispatchR)\n   740\u2192\t}\n   741\u2192\tqueue.nextDispatchR += request.totalWork()\n   742\u2192\treturn true\n   743\u2192}\n   744\u2192\n   745\u2192// canAccommodateSeatsLocked returns true if this queueSet has enough\n   746\u2192// seats available to accommodate a request with the given number of seats,\n   747\u2192// otherwise it returns false.\n   748\u2192func (qs *queueSet) canAccommodateSeatsLocked(seats int) bool {\n   749\u2192\tswitch {\n   750\u2192\tcase qs.qCfg.DesiredNumQueues < 0:\n   751\u2192\t\t// finish time, but\n   755\u2192\t\t// the number of seats this request asks for exceeds the concurrency limit.\n   756\u2192\t\t// TODO: this is a quick fix for now, once we have borrowing in place we will not need it\n   757\u2192\t\tif qs.totRequestsExecuting == 0 {\n   758\u2192\t\t\t// TODO: apply additional lateny associated with this request, as described in the KEP\n   759\u2192\t\t\treturn true\n   760\u2192\t\t}\n   761\u2192\t\t// wait for all \"currently\" executing requests in this queueSet\n   762\u2192\t\t// to finish before we can execute this request.\n   763\u2192\t\treturn 771\u2192// findDispatchQueueToBoundLocked examines the queues in round robin order and\n   772\u2192// returns the first one of those for which the virtual finish time of\n   773\u2192// the oldest waiting request is minimal, and also returns that request.\n   774\u2192// Returns nils if the head of the selected queue can not be dispatched now,\n   775\u2192// in which case the caller does not need to follow up with`qs.boundNextDispatchLocked`.\n   776\u2192func (qs *queueSet) findDispatchQueueToBoundLocked() (*queue, *request) {\n   777\u2192\tminVirtualFinish := fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds\n   778\u2192\tsMin := fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds\n   779\u2192\tdsMin := fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds\n   780\u2192\tsMax := fqrequest.MinSeatSeconds\n   781\u2192\tdsMax := fqrequest.MinSeatSeconds\n   782\u2192\tvar minQueue *queue\n   783\u2192\tvar minIndex int\n   784\u2192\tnq := len(qs.queues)\n   785\u2192\tfor range qs.queues {\n   786\u2192\t\tqs.robinIndex = (qs.robinIndex + 1) % nq\n   787\u2192\t\tqueue := qs.queues[qs.robinIndex]\n   788\u2192\t\toldestWaiting, _ := queue.requestsWaiting.Peek()\n   789\u2192\t\tif oldestWaiting != nil {\n   790\u2192\t\t\tsMin = min(sMin, queue.nextDispatchR)\n   791\u2192\t\t\tsMax = max(sMax, queue.nextDispatchR)\n   792\u2192\t\t\testimatedWorkInProgress := fqrequest.SeatsTimesDuration(float64(queue.seatsInUse), qs.estimatedServiceDuration)\n   793\u2192\t\t\tdsMin = min(dsMin, queue.nextDispatchR-estimatedWorkInProgress)\n   794\u2192\t\t\tdsMax = max(dsMax, queue.nextDispatchR-estimatedWorkInProgress)\n   795\u2192\t\t\tcurrentVirtualFinish := queue.nextDispatchR + oldestWaiting.totalWork()\n   796\u2192\t\t\tklog.V(11).InfoS(\"Considering queue to dispatch\", \"queueSet\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"queue\", 799\u2192\t\t\t\tminQueue = queue\n   800\u2192\t\t\t\tminIndex = qs.robinIndex\n   801\u2192\t\t\t}\n   802\u2192\t\t}\n   803\u2192\t}\n   804\u2192\n   805\u2192\toldestReqFromMinQueue, _ := minQueue.requestsWaiting.Peek()\n   806\u2192\tif oldestReqFromMinQueue == nil {\n   807\u2192\t\t// This cannot happen\n   808\u2192\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"selected queue is empty\"), 815\u2192\t\tif klogV.Enabled() {\n   816\u2192\t\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s): request %v %v seats %d cannot be dispatched from queue %d, waiting for currently executing requests to complete, %d requests 820\u2192\t\treturn nil, nil\n   821\u2192\t}\n   822\u2192\toldestReqFromMinQueue.removeFromQueueLocked()\n   823\u2192\n   824\u2192\t// If the requested final seats exceed capacity of that queue,\n   825\u2192\t// we reduce them to current capacity and adjust additional latency\n   826\u2192\t// to preserve the total amount of work.\n   827\u2192\tif oldestReqFromMinQueue.workEstimate.FinalSeats > uint64(qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit) {\n   828\u2192\t\tfinalSeats := uint64(qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)\n   829\u2192\t\tadditionalLatency := oldestReqFromMinQueue.workEstimate.finalWork.DurationPerSeat(float64(finalSeats))\n   830\u2192\t\toldestReqFromMinQueue.workEstimate.FinalSeats = finalSeats\n   831\u2192\t\toldestReqFromMinQueue.workEstimate.AdditionalLatency = additionalLatency\n   832\u2192\t}\n   833\u2192\n   834\u2192\t// we set the round robin indexing to start at the chose queue\n This way the non-selected queues\n   836\u2192\t// win in the case that the virtual finish times are the same\n   837\u2192\tqs.robinIndex = minIndex\n   838\u2192\n   839\u2192\tif minQueue.nextDispatchR < oldestReqFromMinQueue.arrivalR {\n   840\u2192\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"dispatch before arrival\"), \"Inconceivable!\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"queue\", minQueue.index, \"dispatchR\", minQueue.nextDispatchR, \"request\", oldestReqFromMinQueue)\n   841\u2192\t}\n   842\u2192\tmetrics.SetDispatchMetrics(qs.qCfg.Name, qs.currentR.ToFloat(), minQueue.nextDispatchR.ToFloat(), sMin.ToFloat(), sMax.ToFloat(), dsMin.ToFloat(), dsMax.ToFloat())\n   843\u2192\treturn minQueue, oldestReqFromMinQueue\n   844\u2192}\n   845\u2192\n   846\u2192// finishRequestAndDispatchAsMuchAsPossible is a convenience method\n   847\u2192// which calls finishRequest for a given request and then dispatches\n   848\u2192// as many requests as possible. This\n   862\u2192// callback updates important state in the queueSet\n   863\u2192func (qs *queueSet) finishRequestLocked(r *request) {\n   864\u2192\tnow := qs.clock.Now()\n runtime cost is O(1).\n// The returned value is the element removed, if indeed one was removed,\n// otherwise `nil`.\ntype removeFromFIFOFunc func() *request\n\n// walkFunc is called for each request in the list in the\n// oldest -> newest order.\n// ok: if walkFunc returns false then the iteration stops immediately.\n// walkFunc may remove the given request from the fifo,\n// but may not mutate the fifo in any othe way.\ntype walkFunc func(*request) (ok bool)\n\n// Internal interface to abstract out the implementation details\n// of the underlying list used to maintain the requests.\n//\n// Note that a fifo, including the removeFromFIFOFuncs returned from Enqueue,\n// is not safe for concurrent use by multiple goroutines.\ntype fifo interface {\n\t// Enqueue enqueues the specified request into the list and\n\t// returns a removeFromFIFOFunc function that can be used to remove the\n\t// request from the list\n\tEnqueue(*request) removeFromFIFOFunc\n\n\t// Dequeue pulls out the oldest request from the list.\n\tDequeue() (*request, bool)\n\n\t// Peek returns the oldest request without removing it.\n\tPeek() (*request, bool)\n\n\t// Length returns the number of requests in the list.\n\tLength() int\n\n\t// QueueSum returns the sum of initial seats, final seats, and\n\t// additional latency aggregated from all requests in this queue.\n\tQueueSum() queueSum\n\n\t// Walk function\n\t// stops the walk an returns immediately.\n\tWalk(walkFunc)\n}\n\n// the FIFO list implementation is not safe for concurrent use by multiple\n// goroutines.\ntype requestFIFO struct current = next {\n\t\tnext = current.Next() // f is allowed to remove current\n\t\tif r, ok := current.Value.(*request); ok {\n\t\t\tif !f(r) {\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc *queueSum, req *request) {\n\tsum.InitialSeatsSum -= req.InitialSeats()\n\tsum.MaxSeatsSum -= req.MaxSeats()\n\tsum.TotalWorkSum -= req.totalWork()\n}\n",
